      *================================================================
      * Addition calculation for the EDI OUTPUT
      *================================================================
      * sort factor
     C           TGBEPR    DIV  100       YL0041           Sort Factor
      * Meat value
      * MeatVal Factr Amt/Crc CWT
      * LCL.MeatVal Factr Amt/Crc CWT =
      *    *COMPUTE ((x1 / x2) * x3)
      * x1    : DB1.CD Meat Value Factor Amt
      * /     : PGM.*Synon (15,5) work field *Rounded
      * x2    : DB1.CD Carcass/Hot Weight
      * *     : PGM.*Synon (15,2) work field *Rounded
      * x3    : CON.100
     C           TGIEUF    DIV  TGEWNB    W0WB01    H      *Synon (15,5) w
     C           W0WB01    MULT 100       W0WA00    H      *Synon (15,2) w
     C                     Z-ADDW0WA00    YL0042           MeatVal Factr A
      * fixed cost
      * Fixed Cost Fctr /Crc CWT
      * LCL.Fixed Cost Fctr /Crc CWT =
      *    *COMPUTE ((x1 / x2) * x3)
      * x1    : DB1.CD Fixed Cost Factor Amt
      * /     : PGM.*Synon (15,5) work field *Rounded
      * x2    : DB1.CD Carcass/Hot Weight
      * *     : PGM.*Synon (15,2) work field *Rounded
      * x3    : CON.100
     C           TGORUE    DIV  TGEWNB    W0WB01    H      *Synon (15,5) w
     C           W0WB01    MULT 100       W0WA00    H      *Synon (15,2) w
